SortedAndFixedKeysDict({'generation_step': cms.Path(generator+decayfilterpositiveleg+generatorSmeared,genParticles,genParticlesForJets,genParticlesForJetsNoNu,ak4GenJets,ak8GenJets,ak4GenJetsNoNu,ak8GenJetsNoNu,genCandidatesForMET,genParticlesForMETAllVisible,genMetCalo,genMetTrue,LHCTransport)
})
